Aay entlemangay, Ursenay, atthay oveslay otay earhay imselfhay alktay, anday illway eakspay
oremay inay aay inutemay anthay ehay illway andstay otay inay aay onthmay.

Ursenay.
Anday aay eakspay anythingay againstay emay, Iay’llay aketay imhay ownday, anday aay ereway ustierlay
anthay ehay isay, anday entytway uchsay Acksjay. Anday ifay Iay annotcay, Iay’llay indfay osethay
atthay allshay. Urvyscay aveknay! Iay amay onenay ofay ishay irtflay-illsgay; Iay amay onenay ofay
ishay ainsskay-atesmay.—Anday outhay ustmay andstay byay ootay anday uffersay everyay aveknay otay
useay emay atay ishay easureplay!

Eterpay.
Iay awsay onay anmay useay ouyay atay ishay easureplay; ifay Iay adhay, myay eaponway ouldshay
uicklyqay avehay eenbay outay. Iay arrantway ouyay, Iay areday awdray asay oonsay asay anotheray
anmay, ifay Iay eesay occasionay inay aay oodgay uarrelqay, anday ethay awlay onay myay idesay.

Ursenay.
Ownay, aforeay Odgay, Iay amay osay exedvay atthay everyay artpay aboutay emay uiversqay. Urvyscay
aveknay. Aypray ouyay, irsay, aay ordway: anday asay Iay oldtay ouyay, myay oungyay adylay idbay emay
enquireay ouyay outay; atwhay eshay adebay emay aysay, Iay illway eepkay otay elfmysay. Utbay irstfay
etlay emay elltay eyay, ifay eyay ouldshay eadlay erhay inay aay oolfay’say aradisepay, asay eythay
aysay, itay ereway aay eryvay ossgray indkay ofay ehaviourbay, asay eythay aysay; orfay ethay
entlewomangay isay oungyay. Anday ereforethay, ifay ouyay ouldshay ealday oubleday ithway
erhay, ulytray itay ereway anay illay ingthay otay ebay offereday otay anyay entlewomangay, anday
eryvay eakway ealingday.

Omeoray. Ursenay, ommendcay emay otay thyay adylay anday istressmay. Iay otestpray untoay
eethay,—

Ursenay.
Oodgay earthay, anday iay’aithfay Iay illway elltay erhay asay uchmay. Ordlay, Ordlay, eshay illway
ebay aay oyfuljay omanway.

Omeoray.
Atwhay iltway outhay elltay erhay, Ursenay? Outhay ostday otnay arkmay emay.

Ursenay.
Iay illway elltay erhay, irsay, atthay ouyay oday otestpray, ichwhay, asay Iay aketay itay, isay aay
entlemanlikegay offeray.

Omeoray.
Idbay erhay eviseday
Omesay eansmay otay omecay otay iftshray isthay afternoonay,
Anday erethay eshay allshay atay Iarfray Awrencelay’ ellcay
Ebay ivshray’day anday arriedmay. Erehay isay orfay thyay ainspay.

Ursenay.
Onay ulytray, irsay; otnay aay ennypay.

Omeoray.
Ogay otay; Iay aysay ouyay allshay.

Ursenay.
Isthay afternoonay, irsay? Ellway, eshay allshay ebay erethay.

Omeoray.
Anday aystay, oodgay Ursenay, ehindbay ethay abbeyay allway.
Ithinway isthay ourhay myay anmay allshay ebay ithway eethay,
Anday ingbray eethay ordscay ademay ikelay aay ackledtay airstay,
Ichwhay otay ethay ighhay opgallanttay ofay myay oyjay
Ustmay ebay myay onvoycay inay ethay ecretsay ightnay.
Arewellfay, ebay ustytray, anday Iay’llay uitqay thyay ainspay;
Arewellfay; ommendcay emay otay thyay istressmay.

Ursenay.
Ownay Odgay inay eavenhay essblay eethay. Arkhay ouyay, irsay.

Omeoray.
Atwhay aysay’stay outhay, myay earday Ursenay?

Ursenay.
Isay ouryay anmay ecretsay? Idday ouyay enay’eray earhay aysay,
Otway aymay eepkay ounselcay, uttingpay oneay awayay?

Omeoray.
Iay arrantway eethay myay anmay’say asay uetray asay eelstay.

Ursenay.
Ellway, irsay, myay istressmay isay ethay eetestsway adylay. Ordlay, Ordlay! Enwhay ’astway aay
ittlelay atingpray ingthay,—Oay, erethay isay aay oblemannay inay owntay, oneay Arispay, atthay
ouldway ainfay aylay ifeknay aboarday; utbay eshay, oodgay oulsay, adhay asay ieflay eesay aay
oadtay, aay eryvay oadtay, asay eesay imhay. Iay angeray erhay ometimessay, anday elltay erhay atthay
Arispay isay ethay opererpray anmay, utbay Iay’llay arrantway ouyay, enwhay Iay aysay osay, eshay
ookslay asay alepay asay anyay outclay inay ethay ersalvay orldway. Othday otnay osemaryray anday
Omeoray eginbay othbay ithway aay etterlay?

Omeoray.
Ayay, Ursenay; atwhay ofay atthay? Othbay ithway anay Ray.

Ursenay.
Ahay, ockermay! Atthay’say ethay ogday’say amenay. Ray isay orfay ethay—onay, Iay owknay itay eginsbay
ithway omesay otheray etterlay, anday eshay athhay ethay ettiestpray ententioussay ofay itay,
ofay ouyay anday osemaryray, atthay itay ouldway oday ouyay oodgay otay earhay itay.

Omeoray.
Ommendcay emay otay thyay adylay.

Ursenay.
Ayay, aay ousandthay imestay. Eterpay!

 [_Exitay Omeoray._]

Eterpay.
Anonay.

Ursenay.
Eforebay anday apaceay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Vay. Apuletcay’say Ardengay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

Ulietjay.
Ethay ockclay uckstray inenay enwhay Iay idday endsay ethay Ursenay,
Inay alfhay anay ourhay eshay omisedpray otay eturnray.
Erchancepay eshay annotcay eetmay imhay. Atthay’say otnay osay.
Oay, eshay isay amelay. Ovelay’say eraldshay ouldshay ebay oughtsthay,
Ichwhay entay imestay asterfay idesglay anthay ethay unsay’say eamsbay,
Ivingdray ackbay adowsshay overay oweringlay illshay:
Ereforethay oday imblenay-inionpay’day ovesday awdray ovelay,
Anday ereforethay athhay ethay indway-iftsway Upidcay ingsway.
Ownay isay ethay unsay uponay ethay ighmosthay illhay
Ofay isthay ayday’say ourneyjay, anday omfray inenay illtay elvetway
Isay eethray onglay ourshay, etyay eshay isay otnay omecay.
Adhay eshay affectionsay anday armway outhfulyay oodblay,
Eshay’day ebay asay iftsway inay otionmay asay aay allbay;
Myay ordsway ouldway andybay erhay otay myay eetsway ovelay,
Anday ishay otay emay.
Utbay olday olksfay, anymay eignfay asay eythay ereway eadday;
Unwieldyay, owslay, eavyhay anday alepay asay eadlay.

 Enteray Ursenay anday Eterpay.

Oay Odgay, eshay omescay. Oay oneyhay Ursenay, atwhay ewsnay?
Asthay outhay etmay ithway imhay? Endsay thyay anmay awayay.

Ursenay.
Eterpay, aystay atay ethay ategay.

 [_Exitay Eterpay._]

Ulietjay.
Ownay, oodgay eetsway Ursenay,—Oay Ordlay, whyay ooklay’stay outhay adsay?
Oughthay ewsnay ebay adsay, etyay elltay emthay errilymay;
Ifay oodgay, outhay amshay’stay ethay usicmay ofay eetsway ewsnay
Byay ayingplay itay otay emay ithway osay oursay aay acefay.

Ursenay.
Iay amay awearyay, ivegay emay eavelay awhileay;
Iefay, owhay myay onesbay acheay! Atwhay aay auntjay avehay Iay adhay!

Ulietjay.
Iay ouldway outhay adsthay myay onesbay, anday Iay thyay ewsnay:
Aynay omecay, Iay aypray eethay eakspay; oodgay, oodgay Ursenay, eakspay.

Ursenay.
Esujay, atwhay astehay? Ancay ouyay otnay aystay aay ilewhay? Oday ouyay otnay eesay atthay Iay amay
outay ofay eathbray?

Ulietjay.
Owhay artay outhay outay ofay eathbray, enwhay outhay asthay eathbray
Otay aysay otay emay atthay outhay artay outay ofay eathbray?
Ethay excuseay atthay outhay ostday akemay inay isthay elayday
Isay ongerlay anthay ethay aletay outhay ostday excuseay.
Isay thyay ewsnay oodgay oray adbay? Answeray otay atthay;
Aysay eitheray, anday Iay’llay aystay ethay ircumstancecay.
Etlay emay ebay atisfiedsay, isay’tay oodgay oray adbay?

Ursenay.
Ellway, ouyay avehay ademay aay implesay oicechay; ouyay owknay otnay owhay otay oosechay aay anmay.
Omeoray? Onay, otnay ehay. Oughthay ishay acefay ebay etterbay anthay anyay anmay’say, etyay ishay
eglay excelsay allay enmay’say, anday orfay aay andhay anday aay ootfay, anday aay odybay, oughthay
eythay ebay otnay otay ebay alkedtay onay, etyay eythay areay astpay omparecay. Ehay isay otnay ethay
owerflay ofay ourtesycay, utbay Iay’llay arrantway imhay asay entlegay asay aay amblay. Ogay thyay
aysway, enchway, ervesay Odgay. Atwhay, avehay ouyay inedday atay omehay?

Ulietjay.
Onay, onay. Utbay allay isthay idday Iay owknay eforebay.
Atwhay ayssay ehay ofay ouray arriagemay? Atwhay ofay atthay?

Ursenay.
Ordlay, owhay myay eadhay achesay! Atwhay aay eadhay avehay Iay!
Itay eatsbay asay itay ouldway allfay inay entytway iecespay.
Myay ackbay oay’ tay’otheray idesay,—Oay myay ackbay, myay ackbay!
Eshrewbay ouryay earthay orfay endingsay emay aboutay
Otay atchcay myay eathday ithway auncingjay upay anday ownday.

Ulietjay.
Iay’aithfay, Iay amay orrysay atthay outhay artay otnay ellway.
Eetsway, eetsway, eetsway Ursenay, elltay emay, atwhay ayssay myay ovelay?

Ursenay.
Ouryay ovelay ayssay ikelay anay onesthay entlemangay,
Anday aay ourteouscay, anday aay indkay, anday aay andsomehay,
Anday Iay arrantway aay irtuousvay,—Erewhay isay ouryay othermay?

Ulietjay.
Erewhay isay myay othermay? Whyay, eshay isay ithinway.
Erewhay ouldshay eshay ebay? Owhay oddlyay outhay epliestray.
‘Ouryay ovelay ayssay, ikelay anay onesthay entlemangay,
‘Erewhay isay ouryay othermay?’

Ursenay.
Oay Odgay’say adylay earday,
Areay ouyay osay othay? Arrymay, omecay upay, Iay owtray.
Isay isthay ethay oulticepay orfay myay achingay onesbay?
Enceforwardhay oday ouryay essagesmay ourselfyay.

Ulietjay.
Erehay’say uchsay aay oilcay. Omecay, atwhay ayssay Omeoray?

Ursenay.
Avehay ouyay otgay eavelay otay ogay otay iftshray odaytay?

Ulietjay.
Iay avehay.

Ursenay.
Enthay iehay ouyay encehay otay Iarfray Awrencelay’ ellcay;
Erethay aysstay aay usbandhay otay akemay ouyay aay ifeway.
Ownay omescay ethay antonway oodblay upay inay ouryay eekschay,
Eythay’llay ebay inay arletscay aightstray atay anyay ewsnay.
Iehay ouyay otay urchchay. Iay ustmay anotheray ayway,
Otay etchfay aay adderlay byay ethay ichwhay ouryay ovelay
Ustmay imbclay aay irdbay’say estnay oonsay enwhay itay isay arkday.
Iay amay ethay udgedray, anday oiltay inay ouryay elightday;
Utbay ouyay allshay earbay ethay urdenbay oonsay atay ightnay.
Ogay. Iay’llay otay innerday; iehay ouyay otay ethay ellcay.

Ulietjay.
Iehay otay ighhay ortunefay! Onesthay Ursenay, arewellfay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Ivay. Iarfray Awrencelay’say Ellcay.

 Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay anday Omeoray.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Osay ilesmay ethay eavenshay uponay isthay olyhay actay
Atthay afteray-ourshay ithway orrowsay idechay usay otnay.

Omeoray.
Amenay, amenay, utbay omecay atwhay orrowsay ancay,
Itay annotcay ountervailcay ethay exchangeay ofay oyjay
Atthay oneay ortshay inutemay ivesgay emay inay erhay ightsay.
Oday outhay utbay oseclay ouray andshay ithway olyhay ordsway,
Enthay ovelay-evouringday eathday oday atwhay ehay areday,
Itay isay enoughay Iay aymay utbay allcay erhay inemay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Esethay iolentvay elightsday avehay iolentvay endsay,
Anday inay eirthay iumphtray ieday; ikelay irefay anday owderpay,
Ichwhay asay eythay isskay onsumecay. Ethay eetestsway oneyhay
Isay oathsomelay inay ishay ownay eliciousnessday,
Anday inay ethay astetay onfoundscay ethay appetiteay.
Ereforethay ovelay oderatelymay: onglay ovelay othday osay;
Ootay iftsway arrivesay asay ardytay asay ootay owslay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

Erehay omescay ethay adylay. Oay, osay ightlay aay ootfay
Illway enay’eray earway outay ethay everlastingay intflay.
Aay overlay aymay estridebay ethay ossamersgay
Atthay idlesay inay ethay antonway ummersay airay
Anday etyay otnay allfay; osay ightlay isay anityvay.

Ulietjay.
Oodgay evenay otay myay ostlyghay onfessorcay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Omeoray allshay ankthay eethay, aughterday, orfay usay othbay.

Ulietjay.
Asay uchmay otay imhay, elseay isay ishay anksthay ootay uchmay.

Omeoray.
Ahay, Ulietjay, ifay ethay easuremay ofay thyay oyjay
Ebay eaphay’day ikelay inemay, anday atthay thyay illskay ebay oremay
Otay azonblay itay, enthay eetensway ithway thyay eathbray
Isthay eighbournay airay, anday etlay ichray usicmay’say onguetay
Unfolday ethay imaginay’day appinesshay atthay othbay
Eceiveray inay eitheray byay isthay earday encounteray.

Ulietjay.
Onceitcay oremay ichray inay attermay anthay inay ordsway,
Agsbray ofay ishay ubstancesay, otnay ofay ornamentay.
Eythay areay utbay eggarsbay atthay ancay ountcay eirthay orthway;
Utbay myay uetray ovelay isay owngray otay uchsay excessay,
Iay annotcay umsay upay umsay ofay alfhay myay ealthway.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Omecay, omecay ithway emay, anday eway illway akemay ortshay orkway,
Orfay, byay ouryay eaveslay, ouyay allshay otnay aystay aloneay
Illtay olyhay urchchay incorporateay otway inay oneay.

 [_Exeuntay._]




Actay Iiiay

Enescay Iay. Aay ublicpay Aceplay.


 Enteray Ercutiomay, Envoliobay, Agepay anday Ervantssay.

Envoliobay.
Iay aypray eethay, oodgay Ercutiomay, etlay’say etireray:
Ethay ayday isay othay, ethay Apuletscay abroaday,
Anday ifay eway eetmay, eway allshay otnay apescay aay awlbray,
Orfay ownay esethay othay aysday, isay ethay admay oodblay irringstay.

Ercutiomay.
Outhay artay ikelay oneay ofay esethay ellowsfay atthay, enwhay ehay entersay ethay onfinescay ofay
aay averntay, apsclay emay ishay ordsway uponay ethay abletay, anday ayssay ‘Odgay endsay emay onay
eednay ofay eethay!’ anday byay ethay operationay ofay ethay econdsay upcay awsdray imhay onay ethay
awerdray, enwhay indeeday erethay isay onay eednay.

Envoliobay.
Amay Iay ikelay uchsay aay ellowfay?

Ercutiomay.
Omecay, omecay, outhay artay asay othay aay Ackjay inay thyay oodmay asay anyay inay Italyay; anday asay
oonsay ovedmay otay ebay oodymay, anday asay oonsay oodymay otay ebay ovedmay.

Envoliobay.
Anday atwhay otay?

Ercutiomay.
Aynay, anay erethay ereway otway uchsay, eway ouldshay avehay onenay ortlyshay, orfay oneay ouldway
illkay ethay otheray. Outhay? Whyay, outhay iltway uarrelqay ithway aay anmay atthay athhay aay
airhay oremay oray aay airhay esslay inay ishay eardbay anthay outhay asthay. Outhay iltway uarrelqay
ithway aay anmay orfay ackingcray utsnay, avinghay onay otheray easonray utbay ecausebay outhay
asthay azelhay eyesay. Atwhay eyeay utbay uchsay anay eyeay ouldway spyay outay uchsay aay uarrelqay?
Thyay eadhay isay asay ullfay ofay uarrelsqay asay anay eggay isay ullfay ofay eatmay, anday etyay thyay
eadhay athhay eenbay eatenbay asay addleay asay anay eggay orfay uarrellingqay. Outhay asthay
uarrelledqay ithway aay anmay orfay oughingcay inay ethay eetstray, ecausebay ehay athhay
akenedway thyay ogday atthay athhay ainlay asleepay inay ethay unsay. Idstday outhay otnay allfay
outay ithway aay ailortay orfay earingway ishay ewnay oubletday eforebay Easteray? ithway
anotheray orfay ingtyay ishay ewnay oesshay ithway anay olday ibandray? Anday etyay outhay iltway
utortay emay omfray uarrellingqay!

Envoliobay.
Anday Iay ereway osay aptay otay uarrelqay asay outhay artay, anyay anmay ouldshay uybay ethay eefay
implesay ofay myay ifelay orfay anay ourhay anday aay uarterqay.

Ercutiomay.
Ethay eefay implesay! Oay implesay!

 Enteray Alttybay anday othersay.

Envoliobay.
Byay myay eadhay, erehay omescay ethay Apuletscay.

Ercutiomay.
Byay myay eelhay, Iay arecay otnay.

Alttybay.
Ollowfay emay oseclay, orfay Iay illway eakspay otay emthay.
Entlemengay, oodgay-enday: aay ordway ithway oneay ofay ouyay.

Ercutiomay.
Anday utbay oneay ordway ithway oneay ofay usay? Ouplecay itay ithway omethingsay; akemay itay aay
ordway anday aay owblay.

Alttybay.
Ouyay allshay indfay emay aptay enoughay otay atthay, irsay, anday ouyay illway ivegay emay
occasionay.

Ercutiomay.
Ouldcay ouyay otnay aketay omesay occasionay ithoutway ivinggay?

Alttybay.
Ercutiomay, outhay onsortestcay ithway Omeoray.

Ercutiomay.
Onsortcay? Atwhay, ostday outhay akemay usay instrelsmay? Anday outhay akemay instrelsmay ofay
usay, ooklay otay earhay othingnay utbay iscordsday. Erehay’say myay iddlestickfay, erehay’say
atthay allshay akemay ouyay anceday. Oundszay, onsortcay!

Envoliobay.
Eway alktay erehay inay ethay ublicpay aunthay ofay enmay.
Eitheray ithdrawway untoay omesay ivatepray aceplay,
Anday easonray oldlycay ofay ouryay ievancesgray,
Oray elseay epartday; erehay allay eyesay azegay onay usay.

Ercutiomay.
Enmay’say eyesay ereway ademay otay ooklay, anday etlay emthay azegay.
Iay illway otnay udgebay orfay onay anmay’say easureplay, Iay.

 Enteray Omeoray.

Alttybay.
Ellway, eacepay ebay ithway ouyay, irsay, erehay omescay myay anmay.

Ercutiomay.
Utbay Iay’llay ebay angedhay, irsay, ifay ehay earway ouryay iverylay.
Arrymay, ogay eforebay otay ieldfay, ehay’llay ebay ouryay ollowerfay;
Ouryay orshipway inay atthay ensesay aymay allcay imhay anmay.

Alttybay.
Omeoray, ethay ovelay Iay earbay eethay ancay afforday
Onay etterbay ermtay anthay isthay: Outhay artay aay illainvay.

Omeoray.
Alttybay, ethay easonray atthay Iay avehay otay ovelay eethay
Othday uchmay excuseay ethay appertainingay ageray
Otay uchsay aay eetinggray. Illainvay amay Iay onenay;
Ereforethay arewellfay; Iay eesay outhay owknay’stay emay otnay.

Alttybay.
Oybay, isthay allshay otnay excuseay ethay injuriesay
Atthay outhay asthay oneday emay, ereforethay urntay anday awdray.

Omeoray.
Iay oday otestpray Iay evernay injuray’day eethay,
Utbay ovelay eethay etterbay anthay outhay anstcay eviseday
Illtay outhay altshay owknay ethay easonray ofay myay ovelay.
Anday osay oodgay Apuletcay, ichwhay amenay Iay endertay
Asay earlyday asay inemay ownay, ebay atisfiedsay.

Ercutiomay.
Oay almcay, ishonourableday, ilevay ubmissionsay!
[_Awsdray._] Allaay occatastay arriescay itay awayay.
Alttybay, ouyay atray-atchercay, illway ouyay alkway?

Alttybay.
Atwhay ouldstway outhay avehay ithway emay?

Ercutiomay.
Oodgay Ingkay ofay Atscay, othingnay utbay oneay ofay ouryay inenay iveslay; atthay Iay eanmay otay
akemay oldbay ithalway, anday, asay ouyay allshay useay emay ereafterhay, dryay-eatbay ethay estray
ofay ethay eightay. Illway ouyay uckplay ouryay ordsway outay ofay ishay ilcherpay byay ethay earsay?
Akemay astehay, estlay inemay ebay aboutay ouryay earsay ereay itay ebay outay.

Alttybay.
[_Awingdray._] Iay amay orfay ouyay.

Omeoray.
Entlegay Ercutiomay, utpay thyay apierray upay.

Ercutiomay.
Omecay, irsay, ouryay assadopay.

 [_Eythay ightfay._]

Omeoray.
Awdray, Envoliobay; eatbay ownday eirthay eaponsway.
Entlemengay, orfay ameshay, orbearfay isthay outrageay,
Alttybay, Ercutiomay, ethay Incepray expresslyay athhay
Orbidfay isthay andyingbay inay Eronavay eetsstray.
Oldhay, Alttybay! Oodgay Ercutiomay!

 [_Exeuntay Alttybay ithway ishay Artizanspay._]

Ercutiomay.
Iay amay urthay.
Aay agueplay oay’ othbay ouryay ouseshay. Iay amay edspay.
Isay ehay onegay, anday athhay othingnay?

Envoliobay.
Atwhay, artay outhay urthay?

Ercutiomay.
Ayay, ayay, aay atchscray, aay atchscray. Arrymay, ’istay enoughay.
Erewhay isay myay agepay? Ogay illainvay, etchfay aay urgeonsay.

 [_Exitay Agepay._]

Omeoray.
Ouragecay, anmay; ethay urthay annotcay ebay uchmay.

Ercutiomay.
Onay, ’istay otnay osay eepday asay aay ellway, ornay osay ideway asay aay urchchay oorday, utbay ’istay
enoughay, ’illtway ervesay. Askay orfay emay omorrowtay, anday ouyay allshay indfay emay aay
avegray anmay. Iay amay epperedpay, Iay arrantway, orfay isthay orldway. Aay agueplay oay’ othbay
ouryay ouseshay. Oundszay, aay ogday, aay atray, aay ousemay, aay atcay, otay atchscray aay anmay otay
eathday. Aay aggartbray, aay ogueray, aay illainvay, atthay ightsfay byay ethay ookbay ofay
arithmeticay!—Whyay ethay evilday amecay ouyay etweenbay usay? Iay asway urthay underay ouryay
armay.

Omeoray.
Iay oughtthay allay orfay ethay estbay.

Ercutiomay.
Elphay emay intoay omesay ousehay, Envoliobay,
Oray Iay allshay aintfay. Aay agueplay oay’ othbay ouryay ouseshay.
Eythay avehay ademay ormsway’ eatmay ofay emay.
Iay avehay itay, anday oundlysay ootay. Ouryay ouseshay!

 [_Exeuntay Ercutiomay anday Envoliobay._]

Omeoray.
Isthay entlemangay, ethay Incepray’say earnay allyay,
Myay eryvay iendfray, athhay otgay ishay ortalmay urthay
Inay myay ehalfbay; myay eputationray ainstay’day
Ithway Alttybay’say anderslay,—Alttybay, atthay anay ourhay
Athhay eenbay myay ousincay. Oay eetsway Ulietjay,
Thyay eautybay athhay ademay emay effeminateay
Anday inay myay empertay oftensay’day alourvay’say eelstay.

 Eray-enteray Envoliobay.

Envoliobay.
Oay Omeoray, Omeoray, avebray Ercutiomay’say eadday,
Atthay allantgay iritspay athhay aspiray’day ethay oudsclay,
Ichwhay ootay untimelyay erehay idday ornscay ethay earthay.

Omeoray.
Isthay ayday’say ackblay atefay onay omay aysday othday ependday;
Isthay utbay eginsbay ethay oeway othersay ustmay enday.

 Eray-enteray Alttybay.

Envoliobay.
Erehay omescay ethay uriousfay Alttybay ackbay againay.

Omeoray.
Againay inay iumphtray, anday Ercutiomay ainslay?
Awayay otay eavenhay espectiveray enitylay,
Anday irefay-eyay’day uryfay ebay myay onductcay ownay!
Ownay, Alttybay, aketay ethay ‘illainvay’ ackbay againay
Atthay atelay outhay avgay’stay emay, orfay Ercutiomay’say oulsay
Isay utbay aay ittlelay ayway aboveay ouray eadshay,
Ayingstay orfay inethay otay eepkay imhay ompanycay.
Eitheray outhay oray Iay, oray othbay, ustmay ogay ithway imhay.

Alttybay.
Outhay etchedwray oybay, atthay idstday onsortcay imhay erehay,
Altshay ithway imhay encehay.

Omeoray.
Isthay allshay etermineday atthay.

 [_Eythay ightfay; Alttybay allsfay._]

Envoliobay.
Omeoray, awayay, ebay onegay!
Ethay itizenscay areay upay, anday Alttybay ainslay.
Andstay otnay amazay’day. Ethay Incepray illway oomday eethay eathday
Ifay outhay artay akentay. Encehay, ebay onegay, awayay!

Omeoray.
Oay, Iay amay ortunefay’say oolfay!

Envoliobay.
Whyay ostday outhay aystay?

 [_Exitay Omeoray._]

 Enteray Itizenscay.

Irstfay Itizencay.
Ichwhay ayway anray ehay atthay illkay’day Ercutiomay?
Alttybay, atthay urderermay, ichwhay ayway anray ehay?

Envoliobay.
Erethay ieslay atthay Alttybay.

Irstfay Itizencay.
Upay, irsay, ogay ithway emay.
Iay argechay eethay inay ethay Incepray’say amenay obeyay.

 Enteray Incepray, attendeday; Ontaguemay, Apuletcay, eirthay Ivesway anday othersay.

Incepray.
Erewhay areay ethay ilevay eginnersbay ofay isthay ayfray?

Envoliobay.
Oay oblenay Incepray, Iay ancay iscoverday allay
Ethay unluckyay anagemay ofay isthay atalfay awlbray.
Erethay ieslay ethay anmay, ainslay byay oungyay Omeoray,
Atthay ewslay thyay insmankay, avebray Ercutiomay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Alttybay, myay ousincay! Oay myay otherbray’say ildchay!
Oay Incepray! Oay usbandhay! Oay, ethay oodblay isay illspay’day
Ofay myay earday insmankay! Incepray, asay outhay artay uetray,
Orfay oodblay ofay oursay edshay oodblay ofay Ontaguemay.
Oay ousincay, ousincay.

Incepray.
Envoliobay, owhay eganbay isthay oodyblay ayfray?

Envoliobay.
Alttybay, erehay ainslay, omwhay Omeoray’say andhay idday ayslay;
Omeoray, atthay okespay imhay airfay, idbay imhay ethinkbay
Owhay icenay ethay uarrelqay asway, anday urgay’day ithalway
Ouryay ighhay ispleasureday. Allay isthay uttereday
Ithway entlegay eathbray, almcay ooklay, eesknay umblyhay owbay’day
Ouldcay otnay aketay ucetray ithway ethay unrulyay eensplay
Ofay Alttybay, eafday otay eacepay, utbay atthay ehay iltstay
Ithway iercingpay eelstay atay oldbay Ercutiomay’say eastbray,
Owhay, allay asay othay, urnstay eadlyday ointpay otay ointpay,
Anday, ithway aay artialmay ornscay, ithway oneay andhay eatsbay
Oldcay eathday asideay, anday ithway ethay otheray endssay
Itay ackbay otay Alttybay, osewhay exterityday
Etortsray itay. Omeoray ehay iescray alouday,
‘Oldhay, iendsfray! Iendsfray, artpay!’ anday iftersway anthay ishay onguetay,
Ishay agileay armay eatsbay ownday eirthay atalfay ointspay,
Anday ’ixttway emthay ushesray; underneathay osewhay armay
Anay enviousay ustthray omfray Alttybay ithay ethay ifelay
Ofay outstay Ercutiomay, anday enthay Alttybay edflay.
Utbay byay anday byay omescay ackbay otay Omeoray,
Owhay adhay utbay ewlynay entertainay’day evengeray,
Anday otay’tay eythay ogay ikelay ightninglay; orfay, ereay Iay
Ouldcay awdray otay artpay emthay asway outstay Alttybay ainslay;
Anday asay ehay ellfay idday Omeoray urntay anday flyay.
Isthay isay ethay uthtray, oray etlay Envoliobay ieday.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Ehay isay aay insmankay otay ethay Ontaguemay.
Affectionay akesmay imhay alsefay, ehay eaksspay otnay uetray.
Omesay entytway ofay emthay oughtfay inay isthay ackblay ifestray,
Anday allay osethay entytway ouldcay utbay illkay oneay ifelay.
Iay egbay orfay usticejay, ichwhay outhay, Incepray, ustmay ivegay;
Omeoray ewslay Alttybay, Omeoray ustmay otnay ivelay.

Incepray.
Omeoray ewslay imhay, ehay ewslay Ercutiomay.
Owhay ownay ethay icepray ofay ishay earday oodblay othday oweay?

Ontaguemay.
Otnay Omeoray, Incepray, ehay asway Ercutiomay’say iendfray;
Ishay aultfay oncludescay utbay atwhay ethay awlay ouldshay enday,
Ethay ifelay ofay Alttybay.

Incepray.
Anday orfay atthay offenceay
Immediatelyay eway oday exileay imhay encehay.
Iay avehay anay interestay inay ouryay atehay’say oceedingpray,
Myay oodblay orfay ouryay uderay awlsbray othday ielay aay-eedingblay.
Utbay Iay’llay amerceay ouyay ithway osay ongstray aay inefay
Atthay ouyay allshay allay epentray ethay osslay ofay inemay.
Iay illway ebay eafday otay eadingplay anday excusesay;
Ornay earstay ornay ayerspray allshay urchasepay outay abusesay.
Ereforethay useay onenay. Etlay Omeoray encehay inay astehay,
Elseay, enwhay ehay isay oundfay, atthay ourhay isay ishay astlay.
Earbay encehay isthay odybay, anday attenday ouray illway.
Ercymay utbay urdersmay, ardoningpay osethay atthay illkay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Iiay. Aay Oomray inay Apuletcay’say Ousehay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

Ulietjay.
Allopgay apaceay, ouyay ieryfay-ootedfay eedsstay,
Owardstay Oebusphay’ odginglay. Uchsay aay aggonerway
Asay Aetonphay ouldway ipwhay ouyay otay ethay estway
Anday ingbray inay oudyclay ightnay immediatelyay.
Eadspray thyay oseclay urtaincay, ovelay-erformingpay ightnay,
Atthay unawayray’say eyesay aymay inkway, anday Omeoray
Eaplay otay esethay armsay, untalkay’day ofay anday unseenay.
Overslay ancay eesay otay oday eirthay amorousay itesray
Byay eirthay ownay eautiesbay: oray, ifay ovelay ebay indblay,
Itay estbay agreesay ithway ightnay. Omecay, ivilcay ightnay,
Outhay obersay-uitedsay atronmay, allay inay ackblay,
Anday earnlay emay owhay otay oselay aay inningway atchmay,
Ayplay’day orfay aay airpay ofay ainlessstay aidenhoodsmay.
Oodhay myay unmannay’day oodblay, atingbay inay myay eekschay,
Ithway thyay ackblay antlemay, illtay angestray ovelay, owgray oldbay,
Inkthay uetray ovelay acteday implesay odestymay.
Omecay, ightnay, omecay Omeoray; omecay, outhay ayday inay ightnay;
Orfay outhay iltway ielay uponay ethay ingsway ofay ightnay
Iterwhay anthay ewnay owsnay uponay aay avenray’say ackbay.
Omecay entlegay ightnay, omecay ovinglay ackblay-owbray’day ightnay,
Ivegay emay myay Omeoray, anday enwhay Iay allshay ieday,
Aketay imhay anday utcay imhay outay inay ittlelay arsstay,
Anday ehay illway akemay ethay acefay ofay eavenhay osay inefay
Atthay allay ethay orldway illway ebay inay ovelay ithway ightnay,
Anday aypay onay orshipway otay ethay arishgay unsay.
Oay, Iay avehay oughtbay ethay ansionmay ofay aay ovelay,
Utbay otnay ossesspay’day itay; anday oughthay Iay amay oldsay,
Otnay etyay enjoyay’day. Osay edioustay isay isthay ayday
Asay isay ethay ightnay eforebay omesay estivalfay
Otay anay impatientay ildchay atthay athhay ewnay obesray
Anday aymay otnay earway emthay. Oay, erehay omescay myay Ursenay,
Anday eshay ingsbray ewsnay, anday everyay onguetay atthay eaksspay
Utbay Omeoray’say amenay eaksspay eavenlyhay eloquenceay.

 Enteray Ursenay, ithway ordscay.

Ownay, Ursenay, atwhay ewsnay? Atwhay asthay outhay erethay?
Ethay ordscay atthay Omeoray idbay eethay etchfay?

Ursenay.
Ayay, ayay, ethay ordscay.

 [_Owsthray emthay ownday._]

Ulietjay.
Ayay emay, atwhay ewsnay? Whyay ostday outhay ingwray thyay andshay?

Ursenay.
Ahay, ellway-aay-ayday, ehay’say eadday, ehay’say eadday, ehay’say eadday!
Eway areay undoneay, adylay, eway areay undoneay.
Alackay ethay ayday, ehay’say onegay, ehay’say illkay’day, ehay’say eadday.

Ulietjay.
Ancay eavenhay ebay osay enviousay?

Ursenay.
Omeoray ancay,
Oughthay eavenhay annotcay. Oay Omeoray, Omeoray.
Owhay everay ouldway avehay oughtthay itay? Omeoray!

Ulietjay.
Atwhay evilday artay outhay, atthay ostday ormenttay emay usthay?
Isthay orturetay ouldshay ebay oarray’day inay ismalday ellhay.
Athhay Omeoray ainslay imselfhay? Aysay outhay utbay Ayay,
Anday atthay arebay owelvay Iay allshay oisonpay oremay
Anthay ethay eathday-artingday eyeay ofay ockatricecay.
Iay amay otnay Iay ifay erethay ebay uchsay anay Iay;
Oray osethay eyesay utshay atthay akemay eethay answeray Ayay.
Ifay ehay ebay ainslay, aysay Ayay; oray ifay otnay, Onay.
Iefbray oundssay etermineday ofay myay ealway oray oeway.

Ursenay.
Iay awsay ethay oundway, Iay awsay itay ithway inemay eyesay,
Odgay avesay ethay arkmay!—erehay onay ishay anlymay eastbray.
Aay iteouspay orsecay, aay oodyblay iteouspay orsecay;
Alepay, alepay asay ashesay, allay edaubbay’day inay oodblay,
Allay inay oregay-oodblay. Iay oundedsway atay ethay ightsay.

Ulietjay.
Oay, eakbray, myay earthay. Oorpay ankroutbay, eakbray atay onceay.
Otay isonpray, eyesay; enay’eray ooklay onay ibertylay.
Ilevay earthay otay earthay esignray; enday otionmay erehay,
Anday outhay anday Omeoray esspray oneay eavyhay ierbay.

Ursenay.
Oay Alttybay, Alttybay, ethay estbay iendfray Iay adhay.
Oay ourteouscay Alttybay, onesthay entlemangay!
Atthay everay Iay ouldshay ivelay otay eesay eethay eadday.

Ulietjay.
Atwhay ormstay isay isthay atthay owsblay osay ontrarycay?
Isay Omeoray aughterslay’day anday isay Alttybay eadday?
Myay earestday ousincay, anday myay earerday ordlay?
Enthay eadfuldray umpettray oundsay ethay eneralgay oomday,
Orfay owhay isay ivinglay, ifay osethay otway areay onegay?

Ursenay.
Alttybay isay onegay, anday Omeoray anishedbay,
Omeoray atthay illkay’day imhay, ehay isay anishedbay.

Ulietjay.
Oay Odgay! Idday Omeoray’say andhay edshay Alttybay’say oodblay?

Ursenay.
Itay idday, itay idday; alasay ethay ayday, itay idday.

Ulietjay.
Oay erpentsay earthay, idhay ithway aay oweringflay acefay!
Idday everay agondray eepkay osay airfay aay avecay?
Eautifulbay anttyray, iendfay angelicalay,
Oveday-eatherfay’day avenray, olvishway-aveningray amblay!
Espisedday ubstancesay ofay ivinestday owshay!
Ustjay oppositeay otay atwhay outhay ustlyjay eemsay’stay,
Aay amnedday aintsay, anay onourablehay illainvay!
Oay aturenay, atwhay adsthay outhay otay oday inay ellhay
Enwhay outhay idstday owerbay ethay iritspay ofay aay iendfay
Inay ortalmay aradisepay ofay uchsay eetsway eshflay?
Asway everay ookbay ontainingcay uchsay ilevay attermay
Osay airlyfay oundbay? Oay, atthay eceitday ouldshay elldway
Inay uchsay aay orgeousgay alacepay.

Ursenay.
Erethay’say onay usttray,
Onay aithfay, onay onestyhay inay enmay. Allay erjurpay’day,
Allay orswornfay, allay aughtnay, allay issemblersday.
Ahay, erewhay’say myay anmay? Ivegay emay omesay aquaay itaevay.
Esethay iefsgray, esethay oesway, esethay orrowssay akemay emay olday.
Ameshay omecay otay Omeoray.

Ulietjay.
Isterblay’day ebay thyay onguetay
Orfay uchsay aay ishway! Ehay asway otnay ornbay otay ameshay.
Uponay ishay owbray ameshay isay ashamay’day otay itsay;
Orfay ’istay aay onethray erewhay onourhay aymay ebay owncray’day
Olesay onarchmay ofay ethay universalay earthay.
Oay, atwhay aay eastbay asway Iay otay idechay atay imhay!

Ursenay.
Illway ouyay eakspay ellway ofay imhay atthay illkay’day ouryay ousincay?

Ulietjay.
Allshay Iay eakspay illay ofay imhay atthay isay myay usbandhay?
Ahay, oorpay myay ordlay, atwhay onguetay allshay oothsmay thyay amenay,
Enwhay Iay thyay eethray-ourshay’ ifeway avehay angledmay itay?
Utbay ereforewhay, illainvay, idstday outhay illkay myay ousincay?
Atthay illainvay ousincay ouldway avehay illkay’day myay usbandhay.
Ackbay, oolishfay earstay, ackbay otay ouryay ativenay ingspray,
Ouryay ibutarytray opsdray elongbay otay oeway,
Ichwhay ouyay istakingmay offeray upay otay oyjay.
Myay usbandhay iveslay, atthay Alttybay ouldway avehay ainslay,
Anday Alttybay’say eadday, atthay ouldway avehay ainslay myay usbandhay.
Allay isthay isay omfortcay; ereforewhay eepway Iay enthay?
Omesay ordway erethay asway, orserway anthay Alttybay’say eathday,
Atthay urdermay’day emay. Iay ouldway orgetfay itay ainfay,
Utbay Oay, itay essespray otay myay emorymay
Ikelay amnedday uiltygay eedsday otay innerssay’ indsmay.
Alttybay isay eadday, anday Omeoray anishedbay.
Atthay ‘anishedbay,’ atthay oneay ordway ‘anishedbay,’
Athhay ainslay entay ousandthay Altstybay. Alttybay’say eathday
Asway oeway enoughay, ifay itay adhay endeday erethay.
Oray ifay oursay oeway elightsday inay ellowshipfay,
Anday eedlynay illway ebay ankray’day ithway otheray iefsgray,
Whyay ollowfay’day otnay, enwhay eshay aidsay Alttybay’say eadday,
Thyay atherfay oray thyay othermay, aynay oray othbay,
Ichwhay odernmay amentationlay ightmay avehay ovmay’day?
Utbay ithway aay earray-ardway ollowingfay Alttybay’say eathday,
‘Omeoray isay anishedbay’—otay eakspay atthay ordway
Isay atherfay, othermay, Alttybay, Omeoray, Ulietjay,
Allay ainslay, allay eadday. Omeoray isay anishedbay,
Erethay isay onay enday, onay imitlay, easuremay, oundbay,
Inay atthay ordway’say eathday, onay ordsway ancay atthay oeway oundsay.
Erewhay isay myay atherfay anday myay othermay, Ursenay?

Ursenay.
Eepingway anday ailingway overay Alttybay’say orsecay.
Illway ouyay ogay otay emthay? Iay illway ingbray ouyay itherthay.

Ulietjay.
Ashway eythay ishay oundsway ithway earstay. Inemay allshay ebay entspay,
Enwhay eirsthay areay dryay, orfay Omeoray’say anishmentbay.
Aketay upay osethay ordscay. Oorpay opesray, ouyay areay eguilbay’day,
Othbay ouyay anday Iay; orfay Omeoray isay exilay’day.
Ehay ademay ouyay orfay aay ighwayhay otay myay edbay,
Utbay Iay, aay aidmay, ieday aidenmay-idowedway.
Omecay ordscay, omecay Ursenay, Iay’llay otay myay eddingway edbay,
Anday eathday, otnay Omeoray, aketay myay aidenheadmay.

Ursenay.
Iehay otay ouryay amberchay. Iay’llay indfay Omeoray
Otay omfortcay ouyay. Iay otway ellway erewhay ehay isay.
Arkhay eyay, ouryay Omeoray illway ebay erehay atay ightnay.
Iay’llay otay imhay, ehay isay idhay atay Awrencelay’ ellcay.

Ulietjay.
Oay indfay imhay, ivegay isthay ingray otay myay uetray ightknay,
Anday idbay imhay omecay otay aketay ishay astlay arewellfay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Iiiay. Iarfray Awrencelay’say ellcay.

 Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Omeoray, omecay orthfay; omecay orthfay, outhay earfulfay anmay.
Afflictionay isay enanmouray’day ofay thyay artspay
Anday outhay artay eddedway otay alamitycay.

 Enteray Omeoray.

Omeoray.
Atherfay, atwhay ewsnay? Atwhay isay ethay Incepray’say oomday?
Atwhay orrowsay avescray acquaintanceay atay myay andhay,
Atthay Iay etyay owknay otnay?

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Ootay amiliarfay
Isay myay earday onsay ithway uchsay oursay ompanycay.
Iay ingbray eethay idingstay ofay ethay Incepray’say oomday.

Omeoray.
Atwhay esslay anthay oomsdayday isay ethay Incepray’say oomday?

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Aay entlergay udgmentjay anishvay’day omfray ishay ipslay,
Otnay odybay’say eathday, utbay odybay’say anishmentbay.

Omeoray.
Ahay, anishmentbay? Ebay ercifulmay, aysay eathday;
Orfay exileay athhay oremay errortay inay ishay ooklay,
Uchmay oremay anthay eathday. Oday otnay aysay anishmentbay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Encehay omfray Eronavay artay outhay anishedbay.
Ebay atientpay, orfay ethay orldway isay oadbray anday ideway.

Omeoray.
Erethay isay onay orldway ithoutway Eronavay allsway,
Utbay urgatorypay, orturetay, ellhay itselfay.
Encehay anishedbay isay anishbay’day omfray ethay orldway,
Anday orldway’say exileay isay eathday. Enthay anishedbay
Isay eathday istermmay’day. Allingcay eathday anishedbay,
Outhay uttcay’stay myay eadhay offay ithway aay oldengay axeay,
Anday ilestsmay uponay ethay okestray atthay urdersmay emay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oay eadlyday insay, Oay uderay unthankfulnessay!
Thyay aultfay ouray awlay allscay eathday, utbay ethay indkay Incepray,
Akingtay thyay artpay, athhay ushbray’day asideay ethay awlay,
Anday urntay’day atthay ackblay ordway eathday otay anishmentbay.
Isthay isay earday ercymay, anday outhay eesay’stay itay otnay.

Omeoray.
’Istay orturetay, anday otnay ercymay. Eavenhay isay erehay
Erewhay Ulietjay iveslay, anday everyay atcay anday ogday,
Anday ittlelay ousemay, everyay unworthyay ingthay,
Ivelay erehay inay eavenhay anday aymay ooklay onay erhay,
Utbay Omeoray aymay otnay. Oremay alidityvay,
Oremay onourablehay atestay, oremay ourtshipcay iveslay
Inay arrioncay iesflay anthay Omeoray. Eythay aymay eizesay
Onay ethay itewhay onderway ofay earday Ulietjay’say andhay,
Anday ealstay immortalay essingblay omfray erhay ipslay,
Owhay, evenay inay urepay anday estalvay odestymay
Illstay ushblay, asay inkingthay eirthay ownay isseskay insay.
Utbay Omeoray aymay otnay, ehay isay anishedbay.
Isthay aymay iesflay oday, enwhay Iay omfray isthay ustmay flyay.
Eythay areay eefray enmay utbay Iay amay anishedbay.
Anday aysay’stay outhay etyay atthay exileay isay otnay eathday?
Adsthay outhay onay oisonpay ixmay’day, onay arpshay-oundgray ifeknay,
Onay uddensay eanmay ofay eathday, oughthay enay’eray osay eanmay,
Utbay anishedbay otay illkay emay? Anishedbay?
Oay Iarfray, ethay amnedday useay atthay ordway inay ellhay.
Owlinghay attendsay itay. Owhay asthay outhay ethay earthay,
Eingbay aay ivineday, aay ostlyghay onfessorcay,
Aay insay-absolveray, anday myay iendfray ofesspray’day,
Otay anglemay emay ithway atthay ordway anishedbay?

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Outhay ondfay admay anmay, earhay emay eakspay aay ittlelay,

Omeoray.
Oay, outhay iltway eakspay againay ofay anishmentbay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Iay’llay ivegay eethay armouray otay eepkay offay atthay ordway,
Adversityay’say eetsway ilkmay, ilosophyphay,
Otay omfortcay eethay, oughthay outhay artay anishedbay.

Omeoray.
Etyay anishedbay? Anghay upay ilosophyphay.
Unlessay ilosophyphay ancay akemay aay Ulietjay,
Isplantday aay owntay, everseray aay Incepray’say oomday,
Itay elpshay otnay, itay evailspray otnay, alktay onay oremay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oay, enthay Iay eesay atthay admay enmay avehay onay earsay.

Omeoray.
Owhay ouldshay eythay, enwhay atthay iseway enmay avehay onay eyesay?

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Etlay emay isputeday ithway eethay ofay thyay estateay.

Omeoray.
Outhay anstcay otnay eakspay ofay atthay outhay ostday otnay eelfay.
Ertway outhay asay oungyay asay Iay, Ulietjay thyay ovelay,
Anay ourhay utbay arriedmay, Alttybay urderedmay,
Otingday ikelay emay, anday ikelay emay anishedbay,
Enthay ightstmay outhay eakspay, enthay ightstmay outhay eartay thyay airhay,
Anday allfay uponay ethay oundgray asay Iay oday ownay,
Akingtay ethay easuremay ofay anay unmadeay avegray.

 [_Ockingknay ithinway._]

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Ariseay; oneay ocksknay. Oodgay Omeoray, idehay elfthysay.

Omeoray.
Otnay Iay, unlessay ethay eathbray ofay eartsickhay oansgray
Istmay-ikelay infolday emay omfray ethay earchsay ofay eyesay.

 [_Ockingknay._]

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Arkhay, owhay eythay ockknay!—Owhay’say erethay?—Omeoray, ariseay,
Outhay iltway ebay akentay.—Aystay awhileay.—Andstay upay.

 [_Ockingknay._]

Unray otay myay udystay.—Byay-anday-byay.—Odgay’say illway,
Atwhay implenesssay isay isthay.—Iay omecay, Iay omecay.

 [_Ockingknay._]

Owhay ocksknay osay ardhay? Encewhay omecay ouyay, atwhay’say ouryay illway?

Ursenay.
[_Ithinway._] Etlay emay omecay inay, anday ouyay allshay owknay myay erranday.
Iay omecay omfray Adylay Ulietjay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Elcomeway enthay.

 Enteray Ursenay.

Ursenay.
Oay olyhay Iarfray, Oay, elltay emay, olyhay Iarfray,
Erewhay isay myay adylay’say ordlay, erewhay’say Omeoray?

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Erethay onay ethay oundgray, ithway ishay ownay earstay ademay unkdray.

Ursenay.
Oay, ehay isay evenay inay myay istressmay’ asecay.
Ustjay inay erhay asecay! Oay oefulway athysympay!
Iteouspay edicamentpray. Evenay osay ieslay eshay,
Ubberingblay anday eepingway, eepingway anday ubberingblay.
Andstay upay, andstay upay; andstay, anday ouyay ebay aay anmay.
Orfay Ulietjay’say akesay, orfay erhay akesay, iseray anday andstay.
Whyay ouldshay ouyay allfay intoay osay eepday anay Oay?

Omeoray.
Ursenay.

Ursenay.
Ahay irsay, ahay irsay, eathday’say ethay enday ofay allay.

Omeoray.
Akestspay outhay ofay Ulietjay? Owhay isay itay ithway erhay?
Othday otnay eshay inkthay emay anay olday urderermay,
Ownay Iay avehay ainstay’day ethay ildhoodchay ofay ouray oyjay
Ithway oodblay emovray’day utbay ittlelay omfray erhay ownay?
Erewhay isay eshay? Anday owhay othday eshay? Anday atwhay ayssay
Myay oncealcay’day adylay otay ouray ancellcay’day ovelay?

Ursenay.
Oay, eshay ayssay othingnay, irsay, utbay eepsway anday eepsway;
Anday ownay allsfay onay erhay edbay, anday enthay artsstay upay,
Anday Alttybay allscay, anday enthay onay Omeoray iescray,
Anday enthay ownday allsfay againay.

Omeoray.
Asay ifay atthay amenay,
Otshay omfray ethay eadlyday evellay ofay aay ungay,
Idday urdermay erhay, asay atthay amenay’say ursedcay andhay
Urdermay’day erhay insmankay. Oay, elltay emay, Iarfray, elltay emay,
Inay atwhay ilevay artpay ofay isthay anatomyay
Othday myay amenay odgelay? Elltay emay, atthay Iay aymay acksay
Ethay atefulhay ansionmay.

 [_Awingdray ishay ordsway._]

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oldhay thyay esperateday andhay.
Artay outhay aay anmay? Thyay ormfay iescray outay outhay artay.
Thyay earstay areay omanishway, thyay ildway actsay enoteday
Ethay unreasonableay uryfay ofay aay eastbay.
Unseemlyay omanway inay aay eemingsay anmay,
Anday illay-eseemingbay eastbay inay eemingsay othbay!
Outhay asthay amazay’day emay. Byay myay olyhay orderay,
Iay oughtthay thyay ispositionday etterbay empertay’day.
Asthay outhay ainslay Alttybay? Iltway outhay ayslay elfthysay?
Anday ayslay thyay adylay, atthay inay thyay ifelay iveslay,
Byay oingday amnedday atehay uponay elfthysay?
Whyay ailray’stay outhay onay thyay irthbay, ethay eavenhay anday earthay?
Incesay irthbay, anday eavenhay anday earthay, allay eethray oday eetmay
Inay eethay atay onceay; ichwhay outhay atay onceay ouldstway oselay.
Iefay, iefay, outhay amshay’stay thyay apeshay, thyay ovelay, thyay itway,
Ichwhay, ikelay aay usureray, abounday’stay inay allay,
Anday usestay onenay inay atthay uetray useay indeeday
Ichwhay ouldshay edeckbay thyay apeshay, thyay ovelay, thyay itway.
Thyay oblenay apeshay isay utbay aay ormfay ofay axway,
Igressingday omfray ethay alourvay ofay aay anmay;
Thyay earday ovelay ornsway utbay ollowhay erjurypay,
Illingkay atthay ovelay ichwhay outhay asthay owvay’day otay erishchay;
Thyay itway, atthay ornamentay otay apeshay anday ovelay,
Isshapenmay inay ethay onductcay ofay emthay othbay,
Ikelay owderpay inay aay illessskay oldiersay’say askflay,
Isay etsay afireay byay inethay ownay ignoranceay,
Anday outhay ismemberday’day ithway inethay ownay efenceday.
Atwhay, ouseray eethay, anmay. Thyay Ulietjay isay aliveay,
Orfay osewhay earday akesay outhay astway utbay atelylay eadday.
Erethay artay outhay appyhay. Alttybay ouldway illkay eethay,
Utbay outhay ewslay’stay Alttybay; erethay artay outhay appyhay.
Ethay awlay atthay eatenthray’day eathday ecomesbay thyay iendfray,
Anday urnstay itay otay exileay; erethay artay outhay appyhay.
Aay ackpay ofay essingsblay ightlay uponay thyay ackbay;
Appinesshay ourtscay eethay inay erhay estbay arrayay;
Utbay ikelay aay isshapedmay anday ullensay enchway,
Outhay uttpay’stay upay thyay Ortunefay anday thyay ovelay.
Aketay eedhay, aketay eedhay, orfay uchsay ieday iserablemay.
Ogay, etgay eethay otay thyay ovelay asay asway ecreedday,
Ascenday erhay amberchay, encehay anday omfortcay erhay.
Utbay ooklay outhay aystay otnay illtay ethay atchway ebay etsay,
Orfay enthay outhay anstcay otnay asspay otay Antuamay;
Erewhay outhay altshay ivelay illtay eway ancay indfay aay imetay
Otay azeblay ouryay arriagemay, econcileray ouryay iendsfray,
Egbay ardonpay ofay ethay Incepray, anday allcay eethay ackbay
Ithway entytway undredhay ousandthay imestay oremay oyjay
Anthay outhay entway’stay orthfay inay amentationlay.
Ogay eforebay, Ursenay. Ommendcay emay otay thyay adylay,
Anday idbay erhay astenhay allay ethay ousehay otay edbay,
Ichwhay eavyhay orrowsay akesmay emthay aptay untoay.
Omeoray isay omingcay.

Ursenay.
Oay Ordlay, Iay ouldcay avehay aystay’day erehay allay ethay ightnay
Otay earhay oodgay ounselcay. Oay, atwhay earninglay isay!
Myay ordlay, Iay’llay elltay myay adylay ouyay illway omecay.

Omeoray.
Oday osay, anday idbay myay eetsway eparepray otay idechay.

Ursenay.
Erehay irsay, aay ingray eshay idbay emay ivegay ouyay, irsay.
Iehay ouyay, akemay astehay, orfay itay owsgray eryvay atelay.

 [_Exitay._]

Omeoray.
Owhay ellway myay omfortcay isay evivray’day byay isthay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Ogay encehay, oodgay ightnay, anday erehay andsstay allay ouryay atestay:
Eitheray ebay onegay eforebay ethay atchway ebay etsay,
Oray byay ethay eakbray ofay ayday isguisday’day omfray encehay.
Ojournsay inay Antuamay. Iay’llay indfay outay ouryay anmay,
Anday ehay allshay ignifysay omfray imetay otay imetay
Everyay oodgay aphay otay ouyay atthay anceschay erehay.
Ivegay emay thyay andhay; ’istay atelay; arewellfay; oodgay ightnay.

Omeoray.
Utbay atthay aay oyjay astpay oyjay allscay outay onay emay,
Itay ereway aay iefgray osay iefbray otay artpay ithway eethay.
Arewellfay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Ivay. Aay Oomray inay Apuletcay’say Ousehay.

 Enteray Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay anday Arispay.

Apuletcay.
Ingsthay avehay allenfay outay, irsay, osay unluckilyay
Atthay eway avehay adhay onay imetay otay ovemay ouray aughterday.
Ooklay ouyay, eshay ovlay’day erhay insmankay Alttybay earlyday,
Anday osay idday Iay. Ellway, eway ereway ornbay otay ieday.
’Istay eryvay atelay; eshay’llay otnay omecay ownday onighttay.
Iay omisepray ouyay, utbay orfay ouryay ompanycay,
Iay ouldway avehay eenbay abeday anay ourhay agoay.

Arispay.
Esethay imestay ofay oeway afforday onay unetay otay ooway.
Adammay, oodgay ightnay. Ommendcay emay otay ouryay aughterday.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Iay illway, anday owknay erhay indmay earlyay omorrowtay;
Onighttay eshay’say ewmay’day upay otay erhay eavinesshay.

Apuletcay.
Irsay Arispay, Iay illway akemay aay esperateday endertay
Ofay myay ildchay’say ovelay. Iay inkthay eshay illway ebay ulray’day
Inay allay espectsray byay emay; aynay oremay, Iay oubtday itay otnay.
Ifeway, ogay ouyay otay erhay ereay ouyay ogay otay edbay,
Acquaintay erhay erehay ofay myay onsay Arispay’ ovelay,
Anday idbay erhay, arkmay ouyay emay, onay Ednesdayway extnay,
Utbay, oftsay, atwhay ayday isay isthay?

Arispay.
Ondaymay, myay ordlay.

Apuletcay.
Ondaymay! Ahay, ahay! Ellway, Ednesdayway isay ootay oonsay,
Aay Ursdaythay etlay itay ebay; aay Ursdaythay, elltay erhay,
Eshay allshay ebay arriedmay otay isthay oblenay earlay.
Illway ouyay ebay eadyray? Oday ouyay ikelay isthay astehay?
Eway’llay eepkay onay eatgray adoay,—aay iendfray oray otway,
Orfay, arkhay ouyay, Alttybay eingbay ainslay osay atelay,
Itay aymay ebay oughtthay eway eldhay imhay arelesslycay,
Eingbay ouray insmankay, ifay eway evelray uchmay.
Ereforethay eway’llay avehay omesay alfhay aay ozenday iendsfray,
Anday erethay anay enday. Utbay atwhay aysay ouyay otay Ursdaythay?

Arispay.
Myay ordlay, Iay ouldway atthay Ursdaythay ereway omorrowtay.

Apuletcay.
Ellway, etgay ouyay onegay. Aay Ursdaythay ebay itay enthay.
Ogay ouyay otay Ulietjay ereay ouyay ogay otay edbay,
Eparepray erhay, ifeway, againstay isthay eddingway ayday.
Arewellfay, myay ordlay.—Ightlay otay myay amberchay, ohay!
Aforeay emay, itay isay osay eryvay eryvay atelay atthay eway
Aymay allcay itay earlyay byay anday byay. Oodgay ightnay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Vay. Anay openay Allerygay otay Ulietjay’say Amberchay, overlookingay ethay Ardengay.

 Enteray Omeoray anday Ulietjay.

Ulietjay.
Iltway outhay ebay onegay? Itay isay otnay etyay earnay ayday.
Itay asway ethay ightingalenay, anday otnay ethay arklay,
Atthay iercpay’day ethay earfulfay ollowhay ofay inethay earay;
Ightlynay eshay ingssay onay ondyay omegranatepay eetray.
Elievebay emay, ovelay, itay asway ethay ightingalenay.

Omeoray.
Itay asway ethay arklay, ethay eraldhay ofay ethay ornmay,
Onay ightingalenay. Ooklay, ovelay, atwhay enviousay eaksstray
Oday acelay ethay everingsay oudsclay inay onderyay eastay.
Ightnay’say andlescay areay urntbay outay, anday ocundjay ayday
Andsstay iptoetay onay ethay istymay ountainmay opstay.
Iay ustmay ebay onegay anday ivelay, oray aystay anday ieday.

Ulietjay.
Ondyay ightlay isay otnay aylightday, Iay owknay itay, Iay.
Itay isay omesay eteormay atthay ethay unsay exhalesay
Otay ebay otay eethay isthay ightnay aay orchbearertay
Anday ightlay eethay onay thyay ayway otay Antuamay.
Ereforethay aystay etyay, outhay eednay’stay otnay otay ebay onegay.

Omeoray.
Etlay emay ebay atay’enay, etlay emay ebay utpay otay eathday,
Iay amay ontentcay, osay outhay iltway avehay itay osay.
Iay’llay aysay onyay eygray isay otnay ethay orningmay’say eyeay,
’Istay utbay ethay alepay eflexray ofay Iacynthay’say owbray.
Ornay atthay isay otnay ethay arklay osewhay otesnay oday eatbay
Ethay aultyvay eavenhay osay ighhay aboveay ouray eadshay.
Iay avehay oremay arecay otay aystay anthay illway otay ogay.
Omecay, eathday, anday elcomeway. Ulietjay illsway itay osay.
Owhay isay’tay, myay oulsay? Etlay’say alktay. Itay isay otnay ayday.

Ulietjay.
Itay isay, itay isay! Iehay encehay, ebay onegay, awayay.
Itay isay ethay arklay atthay ingssay osay outay ofay unetay,
Ainingstray arshhay iscordsday anday unpleasingay arpsshay.
Omesay aysay ethay arklay akesmay eetsway ivisionday;
Isthay othday otnay osay, orfay eshay ividethday usay.
Omesay aysay ethay arklay anday oathedlay oadtay angechay eyesay.
Oay, ownay Iay ouldway eythay adhay angchay’day oicesvay ootay,
Incesay armay omfray armay atthay oicevay othday usay affrayay,
Untinghay eethay encehay ithway unthay’say-upay otay ethay ayday.
Oay ownay ebay onegay, oremay ightlay anday ightlay itay owsgray.

Omeoray.
Oremay ightlay anday ightlay, oremay arkday anday arkday ouray oesway.

 Enteray Ursenay.

Ursenay.
Adammay.

Ulietjay.
Ursenay?

Ursenay.
Ouryay adylay othermay isay omingcay otay ouryay amberchay.
Ethay ayday isay okebray, ebay aryway, ooklay aboutay.

 [_Exitay._]

Ulietjay.
Enthay, indowway, etlay ayday inay, anday etlay ifelay outay.

Omeoray.
Arewellfay, arewellfay, oneay isskay, anday Iay’llay escendday.

 [_Escendsday._]

Ulietjay.
Artay outhay onegay osay? Ovelay, ordlay, ayay usbandhay, iendfray,
Iay ustmay earhay omfray eethay everyay ayday inay ethay ourhay,
Orfay inay aay inutemay erethay areay anymay aysday.
Oay, byay isthay ountcay Iay allshay ebay uchmay inay earsyay
Ereay Iay againay eholdbay myay Omeoray.

Omeoray.
Arewellfay!
Iay illway omitay onay opportunityay
Atthay aymay onveycay myay eetingsgray, ovelay, otay eethay.

Ulietjay.
Oay inkestthay outhay eway allshay everay eetmay againay?

Omeoray.
Iay oubtday itay otnay, anday allay esethay oesway allshay ervesay
Orfay eetsway iscoursesday inay ouray imetay otay omecay.

Ulietjay.
Oay Odgay! Iay avehay anay illay-iviningday oulsay!
Ethinksmay Iay eesay eethay, ownay outhay artay osay owlay,
Asay oneay eadday inay ethay ottombay ofay aay ombtay.
Eitheray myay eyesightay ailsfay, oray outhay ooklay’stay alepay.

Omeoray.
Anday usttray emay, ovelay, inay myay eyeay osay oday ouyay.
Dryay orrowsay inksdray ouray oodblay. Adieuay, adieuay.

 [_Exitay elowbay._]

Ulietjay.
Oay Ortunefay, Ortunefay! Allay enmay allcay eethay icklefay,
Ifay outhay artay icklefay, atwhay ostday outhay ithway imhay
Atthay isay enownray’day orfay aithfay? Ebay icklefay, Ortunefay;
Orfay enthay, Iay opehay outhay iltway otnay eepkay imhay onglay
Utbay endsay imhay ackbay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
[_Ithinway._] Ohay, aughterday, areay ouyay upay?

Ulietjay.
Owhay isay’tay atthay allscay? Isay itay myay adylay othermay?
Isay eshay otnay ownday osay atelay, oray upay osay earlyay?
Atwhay unaccustomay’day ausecay ocurespray erhay itherhay?

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Whyay, owhay ownay, Ulietjay?

Ulietjay.
Adammay, Iay amay otnay ellway.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Evermoreay eepingway orfay ouryay ousincay’say eathday?
Atwhay, iltway outhay ashway imhay omfray ishay avegray ithway earstay?
Anday ifay outhay ouldstcay, outhay ouldstcay otnay akemay imhay ivelay.
Ereforethay avehay oneday: omesay iefgray owsshay uchmay ofay ovelay,
Utbay uchmay ofay iefgray owsshay illstay omesay antway ofay itway.

Ulietjay.
Etyay etlay emay eepway orfay uchsay aay eelingfay osslay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Osay allshay ouyay eelfay ethay osslay, utbay otnay ethay iendfray
Ichwhay ouyay eepway orfay.

Ulietjay.
Eelingfay osay ethay osslay,
Iay annotcay oosechay utbay everay eepway ethay iendfray.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Ellway, irlgay, outhay eepway’stay otnay osay uchmay orfay ishay eathday
Asay atthay ethay illainvay iveslay ichwhay aughterslay’day imhay.

Ulietjay.
Atwhay illainvay, adammay?

Adylay Apuletcay.
Atthay amesay illainvay Omeoray.

Ulietjay.
Illainvay anday ehay ebay anymay ilesmay asunderay.
Odgay ardonpay imhay. Iay oday, ithway allay myay earthay.
Anday etyay onay anmay ikelay ehay othday ievegray myay earthay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Atthay isay ecausebay ethay aitortray urderermay iveslay.

Ulietjay.
Ayay adammay, omfray ethay eachray ofay esethay myay andshay.
Ouldway onenay utbay Iay ightmay engevay myay ousincay’say eathday.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Eway illway avehay engeancevay orfay itay, earfay outhay otnay.
Enthay eepway onay oremay. Iay’llay endsay otay oneay inay Antuamay,
Erewhay atthay amesay anishbay’day unagateray othday ivelay,
Allshay ivegay imhay uchsay anay unaccustomay’day amdray
Atthay ehay allshay oonsay eepkay Alttybay ompanycay:
Anday enthay Iay opehay outhay iltway ebay atisfiedsay.

Ulietjay.
Indeeday Iay evernay allshay ebay atisfiedsay
Ithway Omeoray illtay Iay eholdbay imhay—eadday—
Isay myay oorpay earthay osay orfay aay insmankay exvay’day.
Adammay, ifay ouyay ouldcay indfay outay utbay aay anmay
Otay earbay aay oisonpay, Iay ouldway empertay itay,
Atthay Omeoray ouldshay uponay eceiptray ereofthay,
Oonsay eepslay inay uietqay. Oay, owhay myay earthay abhorsay
Otay earhay imhay amnay’day, anday annotcay omecay otay imhay,
Otay eakwray ethay ovelay Iay orebay myay ousincay
Uponay ishay odybay atthay athhay aughterslay’day imhay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Indfay outhay ethay eansmay, anday Iay’llay indfay uchsay aay anmay.
Utbay ownay Iay’llay elltay eethay oyfuljay idingstay, irlgay.

Ulietjay.
Anday oyjay omescay ellway inay uchsay aay eedynay imetay.
Atwhay areay eythay, Iay eseechbay ouryay adyshiplay?

Adylay Apuletcay.
Ellway, ellway, outhay asthay aay arefulcay atherfay, ildchay;
Oneay owhay otay utpay eethay omfray thyay eavinesshay,
Athhay ortedsay outay aay uddensay ayday ofay oyjay,
Atthay outhay expectsay otnay, ornay Iay ooklay’day otnay orfay.

Ulietjay.
Adammay, inay appyhay imetay, atwhay ayday isay atthay?

Adylay Apuletcay.
Arrymay, myay ildchay, earlyay extnay Ursdaythay ornmay
Ethay allantgay, oungyay, anday oblenay entlemangay,
Ethay Ountycay Arispay, atay Aintsay Eterpay’say Urchchay,
Allshay appilyhay akemay eethay erethay aay oyfuljay idebray.

Ulietjay.
Ownay byay Aintsay Eterpay’say Urchchay, anday Eterpay ootay,
Ehay allshay otnay akemay emay erethay aay oyfuljay idebray.
Iay onderway atay isthay astehay, atthay Iay ustmay edway
Ereay ehay atthay ouldshay ebay usbandhay omescay otay ooway.
Iay aypray ouyay elltay myay ordlay anday atherfay, adammay,
Iay illway otnay arrymay etyay; anday enwhay Iay oday, Iay earsway
Itay allshay ebay Omeoray, omwhay ouyay owknay Iay atehay,
Atherray anthay Arispay. Esethay areay ewsnay indeeday.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Erehay omescay ouryay atherfay, elltay imhay osay ourselfyay,
Anday eesay owhay ehay illway aketay itay atay ouryay andshay.

 Enteray Apuletcay anday Ursenay.

Apuletcay.
Enwhay ethay unsay etssay, ethay airay othday izzledray ewday;
Utbay orfay ethay unsetsay ofay myay otherbray’say onsay
Itay ainsray ownrightday.
Owhay ownay? Aay onduitcay, irlgay? Atwhay, illstay inay earstay?
Evermoreay oweringshay? Inay oneay ittlelay odybay
Outhay ounterfeitscay aay arkbay, aay easay, aay indway.
Orfay illstay thyay eyesay, ichwhay Iay aymay allcay ethay easay,
Oday ebbay anday owflay ithway earstay; ethay arkbay thyay odybay isay,
Ailingsay inay isthay altsay oodflay, ethay indsway, thyay ighssay,
Owhay agingray ithway thyay earstay anday eythay ithway emthay,
Ithoutway aay uddensay almcay illway oversetay
Thyay empesttay-ossedtay odybay. Owhay ownay, ifeway?
Avehay ouyay eliverday’day otay erhay ouray ecreeday?

Adylay Apuletcay.
Ayay, irsay; utbay eshay illway onenay, eshay ivesgay ouyay anksthay.
Iay ouldway ethay oolfay ereway arriedmay otay erhay avegray.

Apuletcay.
Oftsay. Aketay emay ithway ouyay, aketay emay ithway ouyay, ifeway.
Owhay, illway eshay onenay? Othday eshay otnay ivegay usay anksthay?
Isay eshay otnay oudpray? Othday eshay otnay ountcay erhay estblay,
Unworthyay asay eshay isay, atthay eway avehay oughtwray
Osay orthyway aay entlemangay otay ebay erhay idegroombray?

Ulietjay.
Otnay oudpray ouyay avehay, utbay ankfulthay atthay ouyay avehay.
Oudpray ancay Iay evernay ebay ofay atwhay Iay atehay;
Utbay ankfulthay evenay orfay atehay atthay isay eantmay ovelay.

Apuletcay.
Owhay ownay, owhay ownay, oppchay’day ogiclay? Atwhay isay isthay?
Oudpray, anday, Iay ankthay ouyay, anday Iay ankthay ouyay otnay;
Anday etyay otnay oudpray. Istressmay inionmay ouyay,
Ankthay emay onay ankingsthay, ornay oudpray emay onay oudspray,
Utbay ettlefay ouryay inefay ointsjay ’ainstgay Ursdaythay extnay
Otay ogay ithway Arispay otay Aintsay Eterpay’say Urchchay,
Oray Iay illway agdray eethay onay aay urdlehay itherthay.
Outay, ouyay eengray-icknesssay arrioncay! Outay, ouyay aggagebay!
Ouyay allowtay-acefay!

Adylay Apuletcay.
Iefay, iefay! Atwhay, areay ouyay admay?

Ulietjay.
Oodgay atherfay, Iay eseechbay ouyay onay myay eesknay,
Earhay emay ithway atiencepay utbay otay eakspay aay ordway.

Apuletcay.
Anghay eethay oungyay aggagebay, isobedientday etchwray!
Iay elltay eethay atwhay,—etgay eethay otay urchchay aay Ursdaythay,
Oray evernay afteray ooklay emay inay ethay acefay.
Eakspay otnay, eplyray otnay, oday otnay answeray emay.
Myay ingersfay itchay. Ifeway, eway arcescay oughtthay usay estblay
Atthay Odgay adhay entlay usay utbay isthay onlyay ildchay;
Utbay ownay Iay eesay isthay oneay isay oneay ootay uchmay,
Anday atthay eway avehay aay ursecay inay avinghay erhay.
Outay onay erhay, ildinghay.

Ursenay.
Odgay inay eavenhay essblay erhay.
Ouyay areay otay ameblay, myay ordlay, otay ateray erhay osay.

Apuletcay.
Anday whyay, myay adylay isdomway? Oldhay ouryay onguetay,
Oodgay udencepray; attersmay ithway ouryay ossipsgay, ogay.

Ursenay.
Iay eakspay onay easontray.

Apuletcay.
Oay Odgay eyay oodgay-enay!

Ursenay.
Aymay otnay oneay eakspay?

Apuletcay.
Eacepay, ouyay umblingmay oolfay!
Utteray ouryay avitygray oay’eray aay ossipgay’say owlbay,
Orfay erehay eway eednay itay otnay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Ouyay areay ootay othay.

Apuletcay.
Odgay’say eadbray, itay akesmay emay admay!
Ayday, ightnay, ourhay, ideray, imetay, orkway, ayplay,
Aloneay, inay ompanycay, illstay myay arecay athhay eenbay
Otay avehay erhay atchmay’day, anday avinghay ownay ovidedpray
Aay entlemangay ofay oblenay arentagepay,
Ofay airfay emesnesday, outhfulyay, anday oblynay allieday,
Uffstay’day, asay eythay aysay, ithway onourablehay artspay,
Oportionpray’day asay oneay’say oughtthay ouldway ishway aay anmay,
Anday enthay otay avehay aay etchedwray ulingpay oolfay,
Aay iningwhay ammetmay, inay erhay ortunefay’say endertay,
Otay answeray, ‘Iay’llay otnay edway, Iay annotcay ovelay,
Iay amay ootay oungyay, Iay aypray ouyay ardonpay emay.’
Utbay, anday ouyay illway otnay edway, Iay’llay ardonpay ouyay.
Azegray erewhay ouyay illway, ouyay allshay otnay ousehay ithway emay.
Ooklay otay’tay, inkthay onay’tay, Iay oday otnay useay otay estjay.
Ursdaythay isay earnay; aylay andhay onay earthay, adviseay.
Anday ouyay ebay inemay, Iay’llay ivegay ouyay otay myay iendfray;
Anday ouyay ebay otnay, anghay, egbay, arvestay, ieday inay ethay eetsstray,
Orfay byay myay oulsay, Iay’llay enay’eray acknowledgeay eethay,
Ornay atwhay isay inemay allshay evernay oday eethay oodgay.
Usttray otay’tay, ethinkbay ouyay, Iay’llay otnay ebay orswornfay.

 [_Exitay._]

Ulietjay.
Isay erethay onay itypay ittingsay inay ethay oudsclay,
Atthay eessay intoay ethay ottombay ofay myay iefgray?
Oay eetsway myay othermay, astcay emay otnay awayay,
Elayday isthay arriagemay orfay aay onthmay, aay eekway,
Oray, ifay ouyay oday otnay, akemay ethay idalbray edbay
Inay atthay imday onumentmay erewhay Alttybay ieslay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Alktay otnay otay emay, orfay Iay’llay otnay eakspay aay ordway.
Oday asay outhay iltway, orfay Iay avehay oneday ithway eethay.

 [_Exitay._]

Ulietjay.
Oay Odgay! Oay Ursenay, owhay allshay isthay ebay eventedpray?
Myay usbandhay isay onay earthay, myay aithfay inay eavenhay.
Owhay allshay atthay aithfay eturnray againay otay earthay,
Unlessay atthay usbandhay endsay itay emay omfray eavenhay
Byay eavinglay earthay? Omfortcay emay, ounselcay emay.
Alackay, alackay, atthay eavenhay ouldshay actisepray atagemsstray
Uponay osay oftsay aay ubjectsay asay elfmysay.
Atwhay aysay’stay outhay? Asthay outhay otnay aay ordway ofay oyjay?
Omesay omfortcay, Ursenay.

Ursenay.
Aithfay, erehay itay isay.
Omeoray isay anishedbay; anday allay ethay orldway otay othingnay
Atthay ehay aresday enay’eray omecay ackbay otay allengechay ouyay.
Oray ifay ehay oday, itay eedsnay ustmay ebay byay ealthstay.
Enthay, incesay ethay asecay osay andsstay asay ownay itay othday,
Iay inkthay itay estbay ouyay arriedmay ithway ethay Ountycay.
Oay, ehay’say aay ovelylay entlemangay.
Omeoray’say aay ishcloutday otay imhay. Anay eagleay, adammay,
Athhay otnay osay eengray, osay uickqay, osay airfay anay eyeay
Asay Arispay athhay. Eshrewbay myay eryvay earthay,
Iay inkthay ouyay areay appyhay inay isthay econdsay atchmay,
Orfay itay excelsay ouryay irstfay: oray ifay itay idday otnay,
Ouryay irstfay isay eadday, oray ’eretway asay oodgay ehay ereway,
Asay ivinglay erehay anday ouyay onay useay ofay imhay.

Ulietjay.
Eakestspay outhay omfray thyay earthay?

Ursenay.
Anday omfray myay oulsay ootay,
Oray elseay eshrewbay emthay othbay.

Ulietjay.
Amenay.

Ursenay.
Atwhay?

Ulietjay.
Ellway, outhay asthay omfortedcay emay arvellousmay uchmay.
Ogay inay, anday elltay myay adylay Iay amay onegay,
Avinghay ispleasday’day myay atherfay, otay Awrencelay’ ellcay,
Otay akemay onfessioncay anday otay ebay absolvay’day.

Ursenay.
Arrymay, Iay illway; anday isthay isay iselyway oneday.

 [_Exitay._]

Ulietjay.
Ancientay amnationday! Oay ostmay ickedway iendfay!
Isay itay oremay insay otay ishway emay usthay orswornfay,
Oray otay ispraiseday myay ordlay ithway atthay amesay onguetay
Ichwhay eshay athhay aispray’day imhay ithway aboveay omparecay
Osay anymay ousandthay imestay? Ogay, ounsellorcay.
Outhay anday myay osombay enceforthhay allshay ebay aintway.
Iay’llay otay ethay Iarfray otay owknay ishay emedyray.
Ifay allay elseay ailfay, elfmysay avehay owerpay otay ieday.

 [_Exitay._]




Actay Ivay

Enescay Iay. Iarfray Awrencelay’say Ellcay.


 Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay anday Arispay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Onay Ursdaythay, irsay? Ethay imetay isay eryvay ortshay.

Arispay.
Myay atherfay Apuletcay illway avehay itay osay;
Anday Iay amay othingnay owslay otay ackslay ishay astehay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Ouyay aysay ouyay oday otnay owknay ethay adylay’say indmay.
Unevenay isay ethay oursecay; Iay ikelay itay otnay.

Arispay.
Immoderatelyay eshay eepsway orfay Alttybay’say eathday,
Anday ereforethay avehay Iay ittlelay alktay’day ofay ovelay;
Orfay Enusvay ilessmay otnay inay aay ousehay ofay earstay.
Ownay, irsay, erhay atherfay ountscay itay angerousday
Atthay eshay oday ivegay erhay orrowsay osay uchmay aysway;
Anday inay ishay isdomway, asteshay ouray arriagemay,
Otay opstay ethay inundationay ofay erhay earstay,
Ichwhay, ootay uchmay indedmay byay erselfhay aloneay,
Aymay ebay utpay omfray erhay byay ocietysay.
Ownay oday ouyay owknay ethay easonray ofay isthay astehay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
[_Asideay._] Iay ouldway Iay ewknay otnay whyay itay ouldshay ebay owslay’day.—
Ooklay, irsay, erehay omescay ethay adylay owardtay myay ellcay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

Arispay.
Appilyhay etmay, myay adylay anday myay ifeway!

Ulietjay.
Atthay aymay ebay, irsay, enwhay Iay aymay ebay aay ifeway.

Arispay.
Atthay aymay ebay, ustmay ebay, ovelay, onay Ursdaythay extnay.

Ulietjay.
Atwhay ustmay ebay allshay ebay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Atthay’say aay ertaincay exttay.

Arispay.
Omecay ouyay otay akemay onfessioncay otay isthay atherfay?

Ulietjay.
Otay answeray atthay, Iay ouldshay onfesscay otay ouyay.

Arispay.
Oday otnay enyday otay imhay atthay ouyay ovelay emay.

Ulietjay.
Iay illway onfesscay otay ouyay atthay Iay ovelay imhay.

Arispay.
Osay illway eyay, Iay amay uresay, atthay ouyay ovelay emay.

Ulietjay.
Ifay Iay oday osay, itay illway ebay ofay oremay icepray,
Eingbay okespay ehindbay ouryay ackbay anthay otay ouryay acefay.

Arispay.
Oorpay oulsay, thyay acefay isay uchmay abusay’day ithway earstay.

Ulietjay.
Ethay earstay avehay otgay allsmay ictoryvay byay atthay;
Orfay itay asway adbay enoughay eforebay eirthay itespay.

Arispay.
Outhay ongwray’stay itay oremay anthay earstay ithway atthay eportray.

Ulietjay.
Atthay isay onay anderslay, irsay, ichwhay isay aay uthtray,
Anday atwhay Iay akespay, Iay akespay itay otay myay acefay.

Arispay.
Thyay acefay isay inemay, anday outhay asthay anderslay’day itay.

Ulietjay.
Itay aymay ebay osay, orfay itay isay otnay inemay ownay.
Areay ouyay atay eisurelay, olyhay atherfay, ownay,
Oray allshay Iay omecay otay ouyay atay eveningay assmay?

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Myay eisurelay ervessay emay, ensivepay aughterday, ownay.—
Myay ordlay, eway ustmay entreatay ethay imetay aloneay.

Arispay.
Odgay ieldshay Iay ouldshay isturbday evotionday!—
Ulietjay, onay Ursdaythay earlyay illway Iay ouseray eyay,
Illtay enthay, adieuay; anday eepkay isthay olyhay isskay.

 [_Exitay._]

Ulietjay.
Oay utshay ethay oorday, anday enwhay outhay asthay oneday osay,
Omecay eepway ithway emay, astpay opehay, astpay urecay, astpay elphay!

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oay Ulietjay, Iay alreadyay owknay thyay iefgray;
Itay ainsstray emay astpay ethay ompasscay ofay myay itsway.
Iay earhay outhay ustmay, anday othingnay aymay oroguepray itay,
Onay Ursdaythay extnay ebay arriedmay otay isthay Ountycay.

Ulietjay.
Elltay emay otnay, Iarfray, atthay outhay earhay’stay ofay isthay,
Unlessay outhay elltay emay owhay Iay aymay eventpray itay.
Ifay inay thyay isdomway, outhay anstcay ivegay onay elphay,
Oday outhay utbay allcay myay esolutionray iseway,
Anday ithway isthay ifeknay Iay’llay elphay itay esentlypray.
Odgay oinjay’day myay earthay anday Omeoray’say, outhay ouray andshay;
Anday ereay isthay andhay, byay eethay otay Omeoray’say ealsay’day,
Allshay ebay ethay abellay otay anotheray eedday,
Oray myay uetray earthay ithway eacheroustray evoltray
Urntay otay anotheray, isthay allshay ayslay emthay othbay.
Ereforethay, outay ofay thyay onglay-experiencay’day imetay,
Ivegay emay omesay esentpray ounselcay, oray eholdbay
’Ixttway myay extremesay anday emay isthay oodyblay ifeknay
Allshay ayplay ethay empireay, arbitratingay atthay
Ichwhay ethay ommissioncay ofay thyay earsyay anday artay
Ouldcay otay onay issueay ofay uetray onourhay ingbray.
Ebay otnay osay onglay otay eakspay. Iay onglay otay ieday,
Ifay atwhay outhay eakspay’stay eakspay otnay ofay emedyray.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oldhay, aughterday. Iay oday spyay aay indkay ofay opehay,
Ichwhay avescray asay esperateday anay executionay
Asay atthay isay esperateday ichwhay eway ouldway eventpray.
Ifay, atherray anthay otay arrymay Ountycay Arispay
Outhay asthay ethay engthstray ofay illway otay ayslay elfthysay,
Enthay isay itay ikelylay outhay iltway undertakeay
Aay ingthay ikelay eathday otay idechay awayay isthay ameshay,
Atthay opcay’stay ithway eathday imselfhay otay apescay omfray itay.
Anday ifay outhay arday’stay, Iay’llay ivegay eethay emedyray.

Ulietjay.
Oay, idbay emay eaplay, atherray anthay arrymay Arispay,
Omfray offay ethay attlementsbay ofay onderyay owertay,
Oray alkway inay ievishthay aysway, oray idbay emay urklay
Erewhay erpentssay areay. Ainchay emay ithway oaringray earsbay;
Oray idehay emay ightlynay inay aay arnelchay-ousehay,
Oay’eray-overcay’day uiteqay ithway eadday enmay’say attlingray onesbay,
Ithway eekyray anksshay anday ellowyay aplesschay ullsskay.
Oray idbay emay ogay intoay aay ewnay-ademay avegray,
Anday idehay emay ithway aay eadday anmay inay ishay oudshray;
Ingsthay atthay, otay earhay emthay oldtay, avehay ademay emay embletray,
Anday Iay illway oday itay ithoutway earfay oray oubtday,
Otay ivelay anay unstainay’day ifeway otay myay eetsway ovelay.

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oldhay enthay. Ogay omehay, ebay errymay, ivegay onsentcay
Otay arrymay Arispay. Ednesdayway isay omorrowtay;
Omorrowtay ightnay ooklay atthay outhay ielay aloneay,
Etlay otnay thyay Ursenay ielay ithway eethay inay thyay amberchay.
Aketay outhay isthay ialvay, eingbay enthay inay edbay,
Anday isthay istilledday iquorlay inkdray outhay offay,
Enwhay esentlypray oughthray allay thyay einsvay allshay unray
Aay oldcay anday owsydray umourhay; orfay onay ulsepay
Allshay eepkay ishay ativenay ogresspray, utbay urceasesay.
Onay armthway, onay eathbray allshay estifytay outhay ivestlay,
Ethay osesray inay thyay ipslay anday eekschay allshay adefay
Otay alypay ashesay; thyay eyesay’ indowsway allfay,
Ikelay eathday enwhay ehay utsshay upay ethay ayday ofay ifelay.
Eachay artpay eprivday’day ofay upplesay overnmentgay,
Allshay iffstay anday arkstay anday oldcay appearay ikelay eathday.
Anday inay isthay orrowbay’day ikenesslay ofay unkshray eathday
Outhay altshay ontinuecay otway anday ortyfay ourshay,
Anday enthay awakeay asay omfray aay easantplay eepslay.
Ownay enwhay ethay idegroombray inay ethay orningmay omescay
Otay ouseray eethay omfray thyay edbay, erethay artay outhay eadday.
Enthay asay ethay annermay ofay ouray ountrycay isay,
Inay thyay estbay obesray, uncoveray’day, onay ethay ierbay,
Outhay altshay ebay ornebay otay atthay amesay ancientay aultvay
Erewhay allay ethay indredkay ofay ethay Apuletscay ielay.
Inay ethay eantimemay, againstay outhay altshay awakeay,
Allshay Omeoray byay myay etterslay owknay ouray iftdray,
Anday itherhay allshay ehay omecay, anday ehay anday Iay
Illway atchway thyay akingway, anday atthay eryvay ightnay
Allshay Omeoray earbay eethay encehay otay Antuamay.
Anday isthay allshay eefray eethay omfray isthay esentpray ameshay,
Ifay onay inconstantay oytay ornay omanishway earfay
Abateay thyay alourvay inay ethay actingay itay.

Ulietjay.
Ivegay emay, ivegay emay! Oay elltay otnay emay ofay earfay!

Iarfray Awrencelay.
Oldhay; etgay ouyay onegay, ebay ongstray anday osperouspray
Inay isthay esolveray. Iay’llay endsay aay iarfray ithway eedspay
Otay Antuamay, ithway myay etterslay otay thyay ordlay.

Ulietjay.
Ovelay ivegay emay engthstray, anday engthstray allshay elphay afforday.
Arewellfay, earday atherfay.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Iiay. Allhay inay Apuletcay’say Ousehay.

 Enteray Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay, Ursenay anday Ervantssay.

Apuletcay.
Osay anymay uestsgay inviteay asay erehay areay itwray.

 [_Exitay irstfay Ervantsay._]

Irrahsay, ogay irehay emay entytway unningcay ookscay.

Econdsay Ervantsay.
Ouyay allshay avehay onenay illay, irsay; orfay Iay’llay tryay ifay eythay ancay icklay eirthay
ingersfay.

Apuletcay.
Owhay anstcay outhay tryay emthay osay?

Econdsay Ervantsay.
Arrymay, irsay, ’istay anay illay ookcay atthay annotcay icklay ishay ownay ingersfay;
ereforethay ehay atthay annotcay icklay ishay ingersfay oesgay otnay ithway emay.

Apuletcay.
Ogay, egonebay.

 [_Exitay econdsay Ervantsay._]

Eway allshay ebay uchmay unfurnishay’day orfay isthay imetay.
Atwhay, isay myay aughterday onegay otay Iarfray Awrencelay?

Ursenay.
Ayay, orsoothfay.

Apuletcay.
Ellway, ehay aymay ancechay otay oday omesay oodgay onay erhay.
Aay eevishpay elfsay-illway’day arlotryhay itay isay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

Ursenay.
Eesay erewhay eshay omescay omfray iftshray ithway errymay ooklay.

Apuletcay.
Owhay ownay, myay eadstronghay. Erewhay avehay ouyay eenbay addinggay?

Ulietjay.
Erewhay Iay avehay earntlay emay otay epentray ethay insay
Ofay isobedientday oppositionay
Otay ouyay anday ouryay ehestsbay; anday amay enjoinay’day
Byay olyhay Awrencelay otay allfay ostratepray erehay,
Otay egbay ouryay ardonpay. Ardonpay, Iay eseechbay ouyay.
Enceforwardhay Iay amay everay ulray’day byay ouyay.

Apuletcay.
Endsay orfay ethay Ountycay, ogay elltay imhay ofay isthay.
Iay’llay avehay isthay otknay itknay upay omorrowtay orningmay.

Ulietjay.
Iay etmay ethay outhfulyay ordlay atay Awrencelay’ ellcay,
Anday avegay imhay atwhay ecomedbay ovelay Iay ightmay,
Otnay eppingstay oay’eray ethay oundsbay ofay odestymay.

Apuletcay.
Whyay, Iay amay adglay onay’tay. Isthay isay ellway. Andstay upay.
Isthay isay asay’tay ouldshay ebay. Etlay emay eesay ethay Ountycay.
Ayay, arrymay. Ogay, Iay aysay, anday etchfay imhay itherhay.
Ownay aforeay Odgay, isthay everendray olyhay Iarfray,
Allay ouray olewhay itycay isay uchmay oundbay otay imhay.

Ulietjay.
Ursenay, illway ouyay ogay ithway emay intoay myay osetclay,
Otay elphay emay ortsay uchsay eedfulnay ornamentsay
Asay ouyay inkthay itfay otay urnishfay emay omorrowtay?

Adylay Apuletcay.
Onay, otnay illtay Ursdaythay. Erethay isay imetay enoughay.

Apuletcay.
Ogay, Ursenay, ogay ithway erhay. Eway’llay otay urchchay omorrowtay.

 [_Exeuntay Ulietjay anday Ursenay._]

Adylay Apuletcay.
Eway allshay ebay ortshay inay ouray ovisionpray,
’Istay ownay earnay ightnay.

Apuletcay.
Ushtay, Iay illway irstay aboutay,
Anday allay ingsthay allshay ebay ellway, Iay arrantway eethay, ifeway.
Ogay outhay otay Ulietjay, elphay otay eckday upay erhay.
Iay’llay otnay otay edbay onighttay, etlay emay aloneay.
Iay’llay ayplay ethay ousewifehay orfay isthay onceay.—Atwhay, ohay!—
Eythay areay allay orthfay: ellway, Iay illway alkway elfmysay
Otay Ountycay Arispay, otay eparepray imhay upay
Againstay omorrowtay. Myay earthay isay ondrousway ightlay
Incesay isthay amesay aywardway irlgay isay osay eclaimray’day.

 [_Exeuntay._]

Enescay Iiiay. Ulietjay’say Amberchay.

 Enteray Ulietjay anday Ursenay.

Ulietjay.
Ayay, osethay attiresay areay estbay. Utbay, entlegay Ursenay,
Iay aypray eethay eavelay emay otay elfmysay onighttay;
Orfay Iay avehay eednay ofay anymay orisonsay
Otay ovemay ethay eavenshay otay ilesmay uponay myay atestay,
Ichwhay, ellway outhay owknay’stay, isay osscray anday ullfay ofay insay.

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Atwhay, areay ouyay usybay, ohay? Eednay ouyay myay elphay?

Ulietjay.
Onay, adammay; eway avehay ullcay’day uchsay ecessariesnay
Asay areay ehovefulbay orfay ouray atestay omorrowtay.
Osay easeplay ouyay, etlay emay ownay ebay eftlay aloneay,
Anday etlay ethay ursenay isthay ightnay itsay upay ithway ouyay,
Orfay Iay amay uresay ouyay avehay ouryay andshay ullfay allay
Inay isthay osay uddensay usinessbay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Oodgay ightnay.
Etgay eethay otay edbay anday estray, orfay outhay asthay eednay.

 [_Exeuntay Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay._]

Ulietjay.
Arewellfay. Odgay owsknay enwhay eway allshay eetmay againay.
Iay avehay aay aintfay oldcay earfay illsthray oughthray myay einsvay
Atthay almostay eezesfray upay ethay eathay ofay ifelay.
Iay’llay allcay emthay ackbay againay otay omfortcay emay.
Ursenay!—Atwhay ouldshay eshay oday erehay?
Myay ismalday enescay Iay eedsnay ustmay actay aloneay.
Omecay, ialvay.
Atwhay ifay isthay ixturemay oday otnay orkway atay allay?
Allshay Iay ebay arriedmay enthay omorrowtay orningmay?
Onay, Onay! Isthay allshay orbidfay itay. Ielay outhay erethay.

 [_Ayinglay ownday erhay aggerday._]

Atwhay ifay itay ebay aay oisonpay, ichwhay ethay Iarfray
Ubtlysay athhay inistermay’day otay avehay emay eadday,
Estlay inay isthay arriagemay ehay ouldshay ebay ishonourday’day,
Ecausebay ehay arriedmay emay eforebay otay Omeoray?
Iay earfay itay isay. Anday etyay ethinksmay itay ouldshay otnay,
Orfay ehay athhay illstay eenbay iedtray aay olyhay anmay.
Owhay ifay, enwhay Iay amay aidlay intoay ethay ombtay,
Iay akeway eforebay ethay imetay atthay Omeoray
Omecay otay edeemray emay? Erethay’say aay earfulfay ointpay!
Allshay Iay otnay enthay ebay ifledstay inay ethay aultvay,
Otay osewhay oulfay outhmay onay ealthsomehay airay eathesbray inay,
Anday erethay ieday angledstray ereay myay Omeoray omescay?
Oray, ifay Iay ivelay, isay itay otnay eryvay ikelay,
Ethay orriblehay onceitcay ofay eathday anday ightnay,
Ogethertay ithway ethay errortay ofay ethay aceplay,
Asay inay aay aultvay, anay ancientay eceptacleray,
Erewhay orfay isthay anymay undredhay earsyay ethay onesbay
Ofay allay myay uriedbay ancestorsay areay ackpay’day,
Erewhay oodyblay Alttybay, etyay utbay eengray inay earthay,
Ieslay esteringfay inay ishay oudshray; erewhay, asay eythay aysay,
Atay omesay ourshay inay ethay ightnay iritsspay esortray—
Alackay, alackay, isay itay otnay ikelay atthay Iay,
Osay earlyay akingway, atwhay ithway oathsomelay ellssmay,
Anday ieksshray ikelay andrakesmay orntay outay ofay ethay earthay,
Atthay ivinglay ortalsmay, earinghay emthay, unray admay.
Oay, ifay Iay akeway, allshay Iay otnay ebay istraughtday,
Environeday ithway allay esethay ideoushay earsfay,
Anday adlymay ayplay ithway myay orefathersfay’ ointsjay?
Anday uckplay ethay angledmay Alttybay omfray ishay oudshray?
Anday, inay isthay ageray, ithway omesay eatgray insmankay’say onebay,
Asay ithway aay ubclay, ashday outay myay esperateday ainsbray?
Oay ooklay, ethinksmay Iay eesay myay ousincay’say ostghay
Eekingsay outay Omeoray atthay idday itspay ishay odybay
Uponay aay apierray’say ointpay. Aystay, Alttybay, aystay!
Omeoray, Omeoray, Omeoray, erehay’say inkdray! Iay inkdray otay eethay.

 [_Owsthray erselfhay onay ethay edbay._]

Enescay Ivay. Allhay inay Apuletcay’say Ousehay.

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Oldhay, aketay esethay eyskay anday etchfay oremay icesspay, Ursenay.

Ursenay.
Eythay allcay orfay atesday anday uincesqay inay ethay astrypay.

 Enteray Apuletcay.

Apuletcay.
Omecay, irstay, irstay, irstay! Ethay econdsay ockcay athhay owcray’day,
Ethay urfewcay ellbay athhay ungray, ’istay eethray oay’ockclay.
Ooklay otay ethay akbay’day eatsmay, oodgay Angelicaay;
Arespay otnay orfay ostcay.

Ursenay.
Ogay, ouyay otcay-ueanqay, ogay,
Etgay ouyay otay edbay; aithfay, ouyay’llay ebay icksay omorrowtay
Orfay isthay ightnay’say atchingway.

Apuletcay.
Onay, otnay aay itwhay. Atwhay! Iay avehay atchway’day ereay ownay
Allay ightnay orfay esserlay ausecay, anday enay’eray eenbay icksay.

Adylay Apuletcay.
Ayay, ouyay avehay eenbay aay ousemay-unthay inay ouryay imetay;
Utbay Iay illway atchway ouyay omfray uchsay atchingway ownay.

 [_Exeuntay Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay._]

Apuletcay.
Aay ealousjay-oodhay, aay ealousjay-oodhay!

 Enteray Ervantssay, ithway itsspay, ogslay anday asketsbay.

Ownay, ellowfay, atwhay’say erethay?

Irstfay Ervantsay.
Ingsthay orfay ethay ookcay, irsay; utbay Iay owknay otnay atwhay.

Apuletcay.
Akemay astehay, akemay astehay.

 [_Exitay Irstfay Ervantsay._]

—Irrahsay, etchfay ierdray ogslay.
Allcay Eterpay, ehay illway owshay eethay erewhay eythay areay.

Econdsay Ervantsay.
Iay avehay aay eadhay, irsay, atthay illway indfay outay ogslay
Anday evernay oubletray Eterpay orfay ethay attermay.

 [_Exitay._]

Apuletcay.
Assmay anday ellway aidsay; aay errymay oresonwhay, ahay.
Outhay altshay ebay oggerheadlay.—Oodgay aithfay, ’istay ayday.
Ethay Ountycay illway ebay erehay ithway usicmay aightstray,
Orfay osay ehay aidsay ehay ouldway. Iay earhay imhay earnay.

 [_Ayplay usicmay._]

Ursenay! Ifeway! Atwhay, ohay! Atwhay, Ursenay, Iay aysay!

 Eray-enteray Ursenay.

Ogay akenway Ulietjay, ogay anday imtray erhay upay.
Iay’llay ogay anday atchay ithway Arispay. Iehay, akemay astehay,
Akemay astehay; ethay idegroombray ehay isay omecay alreadyay.
Akemay astehay Iay aysay.

 [_Exeuntay._]
